CREATE TABLE Users (user_id INT PRIMARY KEY, username VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50))</t><stat>select username, email, device_name from users join sensors on users.user_id = sensors.sensor_id join devices on sensors.device_id = devices.device_id</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE Readings (reading_id INT PRIMARY KEY, reading_value FLOAT, reading_timestamp TIMESTAMP, sensor_id INT REFERENCES Sensors(sensor_id))
